[30;1m12 | [0m[35mbut change detection in hierarchical data is very different from change detection in flat data.[0m
[30;1m13 | [0m[35mXML type formats are also not only used for computer readable data,[0m
[30;1m14 | [0m[35mit is also often used as a format for hierarchical data that can be rendered into human readable for[0m
[30;1m15 | [0m[35mA traditional diff on such a format would tell you line by line the differences,[0m
[30;1m16 | [0m[35mbut this would not be be readable by a human.[0m
[30;1m17 | [0m[35m``xmldiff`` provides tools to make human readable diffs in those situations.[0m
